# JavaScript Data GridGrid Options Reference

<span class="image placeholder _frameworkLogo_192zo_1" original-image-src="https://www.ag-grid.com/_astro/javascript.DOqolN0O.svg" original-image-title="">javascript logo</span>JavaScript<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/ebb52304aa2fe75a94cd1555a353273f67162700.svg" class="lucide lucide-chevron-down _chevronDown_6498a_108" />

Implements the `GridOptions<TData>` interface.

The grid will respond to property updates unless they are marked as `Initial`. See [Updating Grid Options](https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#updating-grid-options).

## Accessories<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-accessories" class="docs-header-icon"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

boolean
default: false

<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">columnMenu<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-accessories-columnMenu" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to columnMenu property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
'legacy' | 'new'
default: 'new'
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
Changes the display type of the column menu. <code>'new'</code> just displays the main list of menu items. <code>'legacy'</code> displays a tabbed menu.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/column-menu/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Column Menu<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressMenuHide<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-accessories-suppressMenuHide" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressMenuHide property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: true
Only recommended for use if <code>columnMenu = 'legacy'</code>. When <code>true</code>, the column menu button will always be shown. When <code>false</code>, the column menu button will only show when the mouse is over the column header. When using <code>columnMenu = 'legacy'</code>, this will default to <code>false</code> instead of <code>true</code>.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/column-menu/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Column Menu<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a></td>
</tr>

<a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/HTMLElement" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">HTMLElement | null</a>
DOM element to use as the popup parent for grid popups (context menu, column menu etc).
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/context-menu/#popup-parent" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Popup Parent<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a></td>

<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />

Resets pivot column order when impacted by filters, data or configuration changes

<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />PivotModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressFieldDotNotation<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-columns-suppressFieldDotNotation" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressFieldDotNotation property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
If <code>true</code>, then dots in field names (e.g. <code>'address.firstLine'</code>) are not treated as deep references. Allows you to use dots in your field name if you prefer.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/value-getters/#field" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Accessing Row Data Values<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a></td>
</tr>

</table>

<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">enterNavigatesVertically<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-editing-enterNavigatesVertically" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to enterNavigatesVertically property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">readOnlyEdit<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-editing-readOnlyEdit" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to readOnlyEdit property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
Set to <code>true</code> to stop the grid updating data after <code>Edit</code>, <code>Clipboard</code> and <code>Fill Handle</code> operations. When this is set, it is intended the application will update the data, eg in an external immutable store, and then pass the new dataset to the grid.<br />
<strong>Note:</strong> <code>rowNode.setDataValue()</code> does not update the value of the cell when this is <code>True</code>, it fires <code>onCellEditRequest</code> instead.

Function
Allows overriding the element that will be focused when the grid receives focus from outside elements (tabbing into the grid). <strong>Returns:</strong> <code>True</code> if this function should override the grid's default behavior, <code>False</code> to allow the grid's default behavior.

<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressColumnVirtualisation<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rendering-suppressColumnVirtualisation" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressColumnVirtualisation property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
Set to <code>true</code> so that the grid doesn't virtualise the columns. For example, if you have 100 columns, but only 10 visible due to scrolling, all 100 will always be rendered. <strong>It is not recommended to set this to <code>true</code> as it may cause performance issues.</strong>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/dom-virtualisation/#suppress-virtualisation" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Suppress Virtualisation<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressRowVirtualisation<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rendering-suppressRowVirtualisation" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressRowVirtualisation property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
Set to <code>true</code> so that the grid doesn't virtualise the rows. For example, if you have 100 rows, but only 10 visible due to scrolling, all 100 will always be rendered. <strong>It is not recommended to set this to <code>true</code> as it may cause performance issues.</strong>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/dom-virtualisation/#suppress-virtualisation" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Suppress Row Virtualisation<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressMaxRenderedRowRestriction<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rendering-suppressMaxRenderedRowRestriction" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressMaxRenderedRowRestriction property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
By default the grid has a limit of rendering a maximum of 500 rows at once (remember the grid only renders rows you can see, so unless your display shows more than 500 rows without vertically scrolling this will never be an issue).<br />
<strong>This is only relevant if you are manually setting <code>rowBuffer</code> to a high value (rendering more rows than can be seen), or <code>suppressRowVirtualisation</code> is true, or if your grid height is able to display more than 500 rows at once.</strong>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/dom-virtualisation/#max-rendered-rows" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Max Rendered Rows<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">enableCellSpan<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rendering-enableCellSpan" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to enableCellSpan property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
When <code>true</code>, enables the cell span feature allowing for the use of the <code>colDef.spanRows</code> property.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/row-spanning/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Row Spanning<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />CellSpanModule</a></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />RowDragModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">rowDragInsertDelay<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rowDragging-rowDragInsertDelay" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to rowDragInsertDelay property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
number
default: 500
Delay in milliseconds. When dragging over, it expands collapsed groups or converts leafs to groups after this delay. Default: <code>500</code>.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/tree-data-row-dragging/#row-drag-insert-delay" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Row Drag Insert Delay<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">isRowValidDropPosition<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rowDragging-isRowValidDropPosition" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to isRowValidDropPosition property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
IsRowValidDropPositionCallback
Called by drag and drop when rows are dragged over another row to conditionally prevent dropping the dragged row on the hovered row. The user can cancel the drop by returning <code>false</code> or customize the operation by returning a <code>IsRowValidDropPositionResult</code>.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />RowDragModule</a></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## Row Grouping<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rowGrouping" class="docs-header-icon"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

See [Row Grouping](https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grouping/) for more information.

<table class="_apiReference_1nt5n_20 _apiReference_119gq_18 no-zebra">
<tbody>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">groupDisplayType<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rowGrouping-groupDisplayType" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to groupDisplayType property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
RowGroupingDisplayType
Specifies how the results of row grouping should be displayed. The options are:
<code>'singleColumn'</code>: single group column automatically added by the grid.
<code>'multipleColumns'</code>: a group column per row group is added automatically.
<code>'groupRows'</code>: group rows are automatically added instead of group columns.
<code>'custom'</code>: informs the grid that group columns will be provided.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grouping-display-types/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Row Grouping - Display Types<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />RowGroupingModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">

## Row Pinning<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rowPinning" class="docs-header-icon"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

Row data uses the [generic type](https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/typescript-generics/) `TData` if provided via `GridOptions<TData>`. Otherwise `TData` will default to `any`.

See [Row Pinning](https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/row-pinning/) for more information.

<table class="_apiReference_1nt5n_20 _apiReference_119gq_18 no-zebra">
<tbody>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">enableRowPinning<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rowPinning-enableRowPinning" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to enableRowPinning property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean | 'top' | 'bottom'
Determines whether manual row pinning is enabled via the row context menu. Set to <code>true</code> to allow pinning rows to top or bottom. Set to <code>'top'</code> to allow pinning rows to the top only. Set to <code>'bottom'</code> to allow pinning rows to the bottom only.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/row-pinning/#enabling-row-pinning" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Row Pinning<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />PinnedRowModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">isRowPinnable<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rowPinning-isRowPinnable" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to isRowPinnable property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
IsRowPinnable
Return <code>true</code> if the grid should allow the row to be manually pinned. Return <code>false</code> if the grid should prevent the row from being pinned When not defined, all rows default to pinnable.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/row-pinning/#preventing-rows-from-being-pinnable" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Row Pinning<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />PinnedRowModule</a></td>

<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">

<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />

Called for every row in the grid. Return "top", "bottom" if the row should be initially pinned to the top or bottom respectively. Return <code>null</code> or <code>undefined</code> otherwise. User interactions can subsequently still change the pinned state of a row.

## Row Pivoting<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rowPivoting" class="docs-header-icon"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

See [Pivoting](https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/pivoting/) for more information.

<table class="_apiReference_1nt5n_20 _apiReference_119gq_18 no-zebra">
<tbody>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">pivotMode<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rowPivoting-pivotMode" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to pivotMode property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
Set to <code>true</code> to enable pivot mode.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/pivoting/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Pivoting<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />PivotModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">pivotPanelShow<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-rowPivoting-pivotPanelShow" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to pivotPanelShow property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
'always' | 'onlyWhenPivoting' | 'never'
default: 'never'
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
When to show the 'pivot panel' (where you drag rows to pivot) at the top. Note that the pivot panel will never show if <code>pivotMode</code> is off.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/pivoting/#enabling-the-pivot-panel" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Enabling the Pivot Panel<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />RowGroupingPanelModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>

number
default: 0
If pivoting, set to the number of column group levels to expand by default, e.g. <code>0</code> for none, <code>1</code> for first level only, etc. Set to <code>-1</code> to expand everything.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/pivoting-column-groups/#expanded-by-default" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Expand Pivot Column Groups by Default<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />PivotModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>

'before' | 'after'

## RowModel: Client-Side<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-clientRowModel" class="docs-header-icon"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

Row data uses the [generic type](https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/typescript-generics/) `TData` if provided via `GridOptions<TData>`. Otherwise `TData` will default to `any`.

<table class="_apiReference_1nt5n_20 _apiReference_119gq_18 no-zebra">
<tbody>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">rowData<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-clientRowModel-rowData" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to rowData property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/typescript-generics/#row-data-tdata" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230" rel="noreferrer" target="_self">TData[] | null</a>
Set the data to be displayed as rows in the grid.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/data-update-row-data/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Updating Row Data<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />ClientSideRowModelModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">resetRowDataOnUpdate<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-clientRowModel-resetRowDataOnUpdate" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to resetRowDataOnUpdate property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
When enabled, getRowId() callback is implemented and new Row Data is set, the grid will disregard all previous rows and treat the new Row Data as new data. As a consequence, all Row State (eg selection, rendered rows) will be reset.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />ClientSideRowModelModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">asyncTransactionWaitMillis<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-clientRowModel-asyncTransactionWaitMillis" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to asyncTransactionWaitMillis property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
number
How many milliseconds to wait before executing a batch of async transactions.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/data-update-high-frequency/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Async transactions<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressModelUpdateAfterUpdateTransaction<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-clientRowModel-suppressModelUpdateAfterUpdateTransaction" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressModelUpdateAfterUpdateTransaction property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
Prevents <a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/data-update-transactions/">Transactions</a> changing sort, filter, group or pivot state when transaction only contains updates. Default: <code>false</code>

## Scrolling<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-scrolling" class="docs-header-icon"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

<table class="_apiReference_1nt5n_20 _apiReference_119gq_18 no-zebra">
<tbody>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">alwaysShowHorizontalScroll<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-scrolling-alwaysShowHorizontalScroll" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to alwaysShowHorizontalScroll property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
Set to <code>true</code> to always show the horizontal scrollbar. Windows and Mac OS both have settings to control scrollbar visibility. Depending on your browser, you may need to adjust the scrollbar settings in your OS to have this property take effect.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">alwaysShowVerticalScroll<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-scrolling-alwaysShowVerticalScroll" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to alwaysShowVerticalScroll property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
Set to <code>true</code> to always show the vertical scrollbar. Windows and Mac OS both have settings to control scrollbar visibility. Depending on your browser, you may need to adjust the scrollbar settings in your OS to have this property take effect.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">debounceVerticalScrollbar<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-scrolling-debounceVerticalScrollbar" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to debounceVerticalScrollbar property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>

</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressHorizontalScroll<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-scrolling-suppressHorizontalScroll" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressHorizontalScroll property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
Set to <code>true</code> to never show the horizontal scroll. This is useful if the grid is aligned with another grid and will scroll when the other grid scrolls. (Should not be used in combination with <code>alwaysShowHorizontalScroll</code>.)
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/aligned-grids/#example-aligned-grid-as-footer" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Aligned Grid as Footer<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressScrollOnNewData<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-scrolling-suppressScrollOnNewData" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressScrollOnNewData property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
When <code>true</code>, the grid will not scroll to the top when new row data is provided. Use this if you don't want the default behaviour of scrolling to the top every time you load new data.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressScrollWhenPopupsAreOpen<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-scrolling-suppressScrollWhenPopupsAreOpen" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressScrollWhenPopupsAreOpen property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
When <code>true</code>, the grid will not allow mousewheel / touchpad scroll when popup elements are present.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressAnimationFrame<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-scrolling-suppressAnimationFrame" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressAnimationFrame property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
When <code>true</code>, the grid will not use animation frames when drawing rows while scrolling. Use this if and only if the grid is working fast enough on all users machines and you want to avoid the temporarily empty rows. <strong>Note:</strong> It is not recommended to set suppressAnimationFrame to <code>true</code> in most use cases as this can seriously degrade the user experience as all cells are rendered synchronously blocking the UI thread from scrolling.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressMiddleClickScrolls<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-scrolling-suppressMiddleClickScrolls" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressMiddleClickScrolls property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
If <code>true</code>, middle clicks will result in <code>click</code> events for cells and rows. Otherwise the browser will use middle click to scroll the grid.<br />
<strong>Note:</strong> Not all browsers fire <code>click</code> events with the middle button. Most will fire only <code>mousedown</code> and <code>mouseup</code> events, which can be used to focus a cell, but will not work to call the <code>onCellClicked</code> function.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressPreventDefaultOnMouseWheel<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-scrolling-suppressPreventDefaultOnMouseWheel" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressPreventDefaultOnMouseWheel property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
If <code>true</code>, mouse wheel events will be passed to the browser. Useful if your grid has no vertical scrolls and you want the mouse to scroll the browser page.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">scrollbarWidth<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-scrolling-scrollbarWidth" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to scrollbarWidth property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
number
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
Tell the grid how wide in pixels the scrollbar is, which is used in grid width calculations. Set only if using non-standard browser-provided scrollbars, so the grid can use the non-standard size in its calculations.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

Theme | 'legacy'
default: themeQuartz
Theme to apply to the grid, or the string "legacy" to opt back into the v32 style of theming where themes were imported as CSS files and applied by setting a class name on the parent element.

<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">

<a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/HTMLElement" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230" rel="noreferrer" target="_blank">HTMLElement</a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
An element to insert style elements into when injecting styles into the grid. If undefined, styles will be added to the document head for grids rendered in the main document fragment, or to the grid wrapper element for other grids (e.g. those rendered in a shadow DOM or detached from the document).</td>

<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">themeCssLayer<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-theme-themeCssLayer" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to themeCssLayer property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
string
The CSS layer that this theme should be rendered onto. If your application loads its styles into a CSS layer, use this to load the grid styles into a previous layer so that application styles can override grid styles.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/theming-css/#css-layers" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">CSS Layers<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">styleNonce<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-theme-styleNonce" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to styleNonce property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
string
The nonce attribute to set on style elements added to the document by themes. If "foo" is passed to this property, the grid can use the Content Security Policy <code>style-src 'nonce-foo'</code>, instead of the less secure <code>style-src 'unsafe-inline'</code>. Note: CSP nonces are global to a page, where a page has multiple grids, every one must have the same styleNonce set.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/security/#style-src" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Security<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a></td>
</tr>

'standard' | 'whenTruncated'
default: `standard`
This defines when tooltip will show up for Cells, Headers and SetFilter Items.
<code>standard</code> - The tooltip always shows up when the items configured with Tooltips are hovered.
<code>whenTruncated</code> - The tooltip will only be displayed when the items hovered have truncated (showing ellipsis) values. This property does not work when <code>enableBrowserTooltips={true}</code>.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />TooltipModule</a></td>

'hover' | 'focus'
default: 'hover'
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
The trigger that will cause tooltips to show and hide.
<code>hover</code> - The tooltip will show/hide when a cell/header is hovered.
<code>focus</code> - The tooltip will show/hide when a cell/header is focused.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />TooltipModule</a></td>

boolean
default: false
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
Set to <code>true</code> to enable tooltip interaction. When this option is enabled, the tooltip will not hide while the tooltip itself it being hovered or has focus.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/tooltips/#interactive-tooltips" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Interactive Tooltips<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />TooltipModule</a></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## Tree Data<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-treeData" class="docs-header-icon"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

Tree Data provides a way to supply the grid with structured hierarchical data.

See [Tree Data](https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/tree-data/) for more information.

<table class="_apiReference_1nt5n_20 _apiReference_119gq_18 no-zebra">
<tbody>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">treeData<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-treeData-treeData" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to treeData property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
Set to <code>true</code> to enable the Grid to work with Tree Data. You must also implement the <code>getDataPath(data)</code> callback.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/tree-data/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Tree Data<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />TreeDataModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">getDataPath<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-treeData-getDataPath" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to getDataPath property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
GetDataPath
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>
Callback to be used when working with Tree Data when <code>treeData = true</code>.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/tree-data/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Tree Data<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />TreeDataModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">treeDataChildrenField<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-treeData-treeDataChildrenField" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to treeDataChildrenField property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
string
The name of the field to use in a data item to retrieve the array of children nodes of a node when while using treeData=true. It supports accessing nested fields using the dot notation.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/tree-data/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Tree Data<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />TreeDataModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">treeDataParentIdField<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-treeData-treeDataParentIdField" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to treeDataParentIdField property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
string
The name of the field to use in a data item to find the parent node of a node when using treeData=true. The tree will be constructed via relationships between nodes using this field. getRowId callback need to be provided as well for this to work. It supports accessing nested fields using the dot notation.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/tree-data/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Tree Data<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />TreeDataModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">autoGroupColumnDef<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-treeData-autoGroupColumnDef" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to autoGroupColumnDef property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/column-properties/" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230" rel="noreferrer" target="_self">ColDef</a>
Allows specifying the group 'auto column' if you are not happy with the default. If grouping, this column definition is included as the first column in the grid. If not grouping, this column is not included.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grouping-single-group-column/#configuration" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Group Column Configuration<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />TreeDataModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">groupDefaultExpanded<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-treeData-groupDefaultExpanded" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to groupDefaultExpanded property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
number
default: 0
If grouping, set to the number of levels to expand by default, e.g. <code>0</code> for none, <code>1</code> for first level only, etc. Set to <code>-1</code> to expand everything.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grouping-opening-groups/#expanding-by-group-level" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Opening Group Levels by Default<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />TreeDataModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">isGroupOpenByDefault<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-treeData-isGroupOpenByDefault" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to isGroupOpenByDefault property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
(Client-side Row Model only) Allows groups to be open by default.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grouping-opening-groups/#expanding-via-callback" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Open Groups by Default<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />TreeDataModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">suppressGroupRowsSticky<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-options/#reference-treeData-suppressGroupRowsSticky" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to suppressGroupRowsSticky property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
boolean
default: false
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-interface/#initial-grid-options" class="_metaValue_1nt5n_230">Initial</a>

<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grouping-opening-groups/#prevent-sticky-groups" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Suppressing Sticky Groups<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-options/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
